add_namespace = sgs
country_event = {
	#军营冲突
	id = sgs.1
	title = sgs.1.t
	desc = sgs.1.d
	fire_only_once = no
	is_triggered_only = no
	immediate = {

	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 120
		modifier = {
			add = -45
			date < 146.6.1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.4
			check_variable = {
				sgs_uprise < 40
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			has_stability > -0.2
		}
	}
	trigger = {
		#date > 146.6.1
		tag = SGS
		#has_stability < 0.2
		#has_war_support > 0.5
		not = {
			SGS_restless_stage_is_over = yes
			has_war = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		#不管
		name = sgs.1.1
		custom_effect_tooltip = up_sgs_uprise
		add_to_variable = {
			sgs_uprise = 5
		}
		clamp_variable = {
			var = sgs_uprise
			min = 1
			max = 150
		}
		add_political_power = 30
		ai_chance = {
			base = 35
		}
	}
	option = {
		#发点武器
		name = sgs.1.2
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = magic_core_a
			amount = -60
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_equipment = {
					magic_core_a < 59
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	#开战
	id = sgs.2
	title = sgs.2.t
	desc = sgs.2.d
	fire_only_once = no
	is_triggered_only = no
	immediate = {
		subtract_from_variable = {
			sgs_uprise = 10
		}
		clamp_variable = {
			var = sgs_uprise
			min = 1
			max = 150
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_decision = SGS_dannmakugokko_deci
			remove_decision = SGS_itazura_deci
			remove_decision = SGS_bettle_arena_deci
			remove_decision = SGS_training_deci
			remove_decision = SGS_show_power_deci
			remove_decision = SGS_producing_war_deci
			remove_decision = SGS_picking_up_deci
			remove_decision = SGS_accept_now_deci

		}

		#remove_mission = SGS_war_promise_deci
		clr_country_flag = sgs_selected_battle_fairy_deci
		clr_country_flag = sgs_deci_doing
		clr_country_flag = sgs_dannmakugokko_unhappy
		set_country_flag = sgs_events_interrupted
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	trigger = {
		tag = SGS
		has_idea = SGS_battle_fairy_restlessness_idea
		has_war = yes
		not = {
			has_country_flag = SGS_civil_war_start
		}
	}
	option = {
		#革命
		name = sgs.2.1
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_exhaustion_lowing_by_battle_fairy
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = SGS_battle_fairy_restlessness_idea
			add_idea = SGS_battle_fairy_restlessness_at_war_idea
		}
		set_country_flag = EXHC_lowing_battle_fairy
		ai_chance = {
			base = 35
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	#要求打仗
	id = sgs.4
	title = sgs.4.t
	desc = sgs.4.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = no
	immediate = {
		add_to_variable = {
			sgs_uprise = 10
		}
		clamp_variable = {
			var = sgs_uprise
			min = 1
			max = 150
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	trigger = {
		or = {
			date > 146.6.1
			has_completed_focus = SGS_drill_in_the_mountain_focus
		}
		tag = SGS
		has_war_support > 0.7
		neworder > 0.5
		not = {
			has_country_flag = sgs_promise_to_BaF
		}
	}
	option = {
		#承诺
		name = sgs.4.1
		custom_effect_tooltip = down_sgs_uprise_little
		subtract_from_variable = {
			sgs_uprise = 5
		}
		clamp_variable = {
			var = sgs_uprise
			min = 1
			max = 150
		}
		add_war_support = 0.05
		add_political_power = 20
		set_country_flag = sgs_promise_to_BaF
		activate_mission = SGS_war_promise_deci
		ai_chance = {
			base = 35
			modifier = {
				neworder > 85
				has_war_support > 0.85
				factor = 2
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#不承诺
		name = sgs.4.2
		custom_effect_tooltip = up_sgs_uprise
		add_to_variable = {
			sgs_uprise = 15
		}
		clamp_variable = {
			var = sgs_uprise
			min = 1
			max = 150
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_war_support = -0.05
		add_political_power = 20
		ai_chance = {
			base = 35
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	#食言
	id = sgs.5
	title = sgs.5.t
	desc ={
		text =  sgs.5.d
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				sgs_uprise < 100
			}
		}
	}
	desc ={
		text =  sgs.5.d_cw
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				sgs_uprise > 99
			}
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = no
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
	}
	#mean_time_to_happen = {
	#	days = 30
	#}
	trigger = {
		tag = SGS
	}
	option = {
		#不爽
		name = sgs.5.1
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				sgs_uprise < 100
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.2
		add_political_power = -20
		custom_effect_tooltip = up_sgs_uprise
		add_to_variable = {
			sgs_uprise = 10
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			sgs_uprise = 1.5
		}
		clamp_variable = {
			var = sgs_uprise
			min = 1
			max = 150
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					sgs_uprise > 100
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = SGS_civil_war_from_war_promise
			country_event = {
				id = sgs.6
				days = 3
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 35
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = sgs.5.2 #直接内战
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				sgs_uprise > 99
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = SGS_civil_war_from_war_promise
		country_event = {
			id = sgs.6
		}

	}
}

country_event = {
	#内战爆发
	id = sgs.6
	title = sgs.6.t
	desc = sgs.6.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
	}
	#mean_time_to_happen = {
	#	days = 30
	#}
	trigger = {
		tag = SGS
	}
	option = {
		#革命
		name = sgs.6.1
		trigger = {

		}
		add_research_slot = -1
		hidden_effect = {

			remove_ideas = SGS_battle_fairy_restlessness_idea
			remove_decision = SGS_dannmakugokko_deci
			remove_decision = SGS_itazura_deci
			remove_decision = SGS_bettle_arena_deci
			remove_decision = SGS_training_deci
			remove_decision = SGS_show_power_deci
			remove_decision = SGS_producing_war_deci
			remove_decision = SGS_picking_up_deci
			remove_decision = SGS_accept_now_deci
			remove_decision = SGS_producing_war_deci
			clear_variable = sgs_uprise
			clr_country_flag = sgs_deci_doing
			clr_country_flag = sgs_selected_battle_fairy_deci
			clr_country_flag = sgs_dannmakugokko_unhappy
			set_country_flag = sgs_events_interrupted
			
			SGS_init_hawk_dove_value = yes
			BAF = {
				add_timed_idea = { idea = panluantouxiang_idea days = 360 }
				add_ideas = {BAF_strong_army_idea  BAF_ingore_product_idea}
				create_field_marshal = {
					name = "贝特尔"
					portrait_path = "gfx/leaders/gen/fai1.dds"
					traits = { trait_reckless }
					skill = 2
					attack_skill = 3
					defense_skill = 1
					planning_skill = 2
					logistics_skill = 1
				}
				set_technology = { BAF_bunker_attck_tech = 1 }
				transfer_state = 116
				transfer_state = 117
				transfer_state = 131
				transfer_state = 376
				transfer_state = 93
				inherit_technology = SGS
				load_oob = BAF_rebel
			}
			BAF = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = SGS
					type = civil_war
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = SGS
				}
				add_core_of = BAF
			}
			set_country_flag = SGS_civil_war_start #标记内战开始

			if = {
				limit = {
					or = {
						and = {
							has_country_flag = SGS_select_fairy_shrine
							not = {has_country_flag = SGS_select_fairy_shrine_over}
						}
						and = {
							has_country_flag = SGS_select_fairy_diplo
							not = {has_completed_focus = SGS_trade_with_other_fairy_focus}
						}
						and = {
							has_country_flag = SGS_select_IN
							not= {
								or = {
									has_country_flag = SGS_IN_failed
									has_completed_focus = SGS_trade_about_industry_focus
								}
							}

						}

					}

				}
				country_event = {
					id = sgs.1051
				}
			}
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
			news_event = {
				id = sgs.106
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 35
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	#开战派煽动
	id = sgs.12
	title = sgs.12.t
	desc = sgs.12.d
	fire_only_once = no
	is_triggered_only = no
	immediate = {

	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 50
		modifier = {
			add = -10
			check_variable = {
				sgs_uprise < 20
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			has_war_support > 0.7
		}
	}
	trigger = {
		not = {
			SGS_restless_stage_is_over = yes
			has_country_flag = SGS_war_won
			has_war = yes
		}
		tag = SGS

	title = sgs.107.t
	desc = sgs.107.d
	fire_only_once = no
	is_triggered_only = yes
	timeout_days = 2
	trigger = {
	}
	immediate = {
	}
	option = {
		#河童
		name = sgs.107.1
		trigger = {
			is_neighbor_of = NTR
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			sgs_sunny_infl = 7
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = neworder
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		#按概率触发事件 30*24=720
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = {
				ROOT.sgs_itazura_target = NTR.id
			}
			random_list = {
				40 = {
					var:ROOT.sgs_itazura_target = {
						country_event = {
							id = sgs.112							#看情况
							days = 10
						}
					}
				}
				10 = {
					#成功
					country_event = {
						id = sgs.110
						days = 20
					}
				}
				50 = {
					country_event = {
						#失败
						id = sgs.108
						days = 20
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 35
		}
	}
	option = {
		#人类
		name = sgs.107.2
		trigger = {
			or = {
				is_neighbor_of = WHM
				is_neighbor_of = HU1
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			sgs_star_infl = 5
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = guli
			popularity = 0.04
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_neighbor_of = WHM
			}
			set_variable = {
				ROOT.sgs_itazura_target = WHM.id
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_neighbor_of = HU1
			}
			set_variable = {
				ROOT.sgs_itazura_target = HU1.id
			}
		}
		#按概率触发事件 30*24=720
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					var:ROOT.sgs_itazura_target = {
						country_event = {
							id = sgs.113							#看情况
							days = 10
						}
					}
				}
				55 = {
					#成功
					country_event = {
						id = sgs.110
						days = 20
					}
				}
				20 = {
					country_event = {
						#失败
						id = sgs.108
						days = 20
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 35
		}
	}
	option = {
		#红魔馆
		name = sgs.107.3
		trigger = {
			is_neighbor_of = SCA
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			sgs_luna_infl = 5
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = oldorder
			popularity = 0.08
		}
		#按概率触发事件 30*24=720
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = {
				ROOT.sgs_itazura_target = SCA.id
			}
			random_list = {
				20 = {
					country_event = {
						id = sgs.115						#罢工
						days = 10
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						oldorder < 0.25
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						SCA = {
							not = {
								has_idea = Fairy
							}
						}
					}
				}
				50 = {
					#成功
					country_event = {
						id = sgs.110
						days = 20
					}
				}
				30 = {
					country_event = {
						#失败
						id = sgs.108
						days = 20
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 35
		}
	}
}

	#恶作剧失败-SGS

	desc = {
		text = sgs.108.d
		trigger = {
			var:ROOT.sgs_itazura_target = {
				OR = {
					original_tag = NTR
					original_tag = SCA
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = sgs.108.d_human
		trigger = {
			var:ROOT.sgs_itazura_target = {
				OR = {
					original_tag = WHM
					original_tag = HU1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = no
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		not = {
			has_country_flag = sgs_events_interrupted
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		clr_country_flag = sgs_selected_battle_fairy_deci
	}
	option = {
		#河童or红魔失败后果
		name = sgs.108.1
		trigger = {
			var:ROOT.sgs_itazura_target = {
				OR = {
					original_tag = NTR
					original_tag = SCA
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = up_sgs_uprise
		add_to_variable = {
			sgs_uprise = 5
		}
		clamp_variable = {
			var = sgs_uprise
			min = 1
			max = 150
		}
		add_stability = -0.03
		add_war_support = -0.05
		var:ROOT.sgs_itazura_target = {
			country_event = {
				id = sgs.109
			}
		}
		clear_variable = ROOT.sgs_itazura_target
		ai_chance = {
			base = 35
		}
	}
	option = {
		#人类失败后果
		name = sgs.108.2
		trigger = {
			var:ROOT.sgs_itazura_target = {
				OR = {
					original_tag = WHM
					original_tag = HU1
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = up_sgs_uprise
		add_to_variable = {
			sgs_uprise = 5
		}
		clamp_variable = {
			var = sgs_uprise
			min = 1
			max = 150
		}
		add_stability = -0.1
		add_war_support = -0.1
		add_manpower = -10
		var:ROOT.sgs_itazura_target = {
			country_event = {
				id = sgs.109
			}
			ROOT = {
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = PREV
					modifier = AKI_shayaojingfan_op
				}
			}
		}
		clear_variable = ROOT.sgs_itazura_target
		ai_chance = {
			base = 35
		}
	}

country_event = {
	#斗技大会开幕
	id = sgs.116
	title = sgs.116.t
	desc = sgs.116.d
	timeout_days = 2
	fire_only_once = no
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		not = {
			has_country_flag = sgs_events_interrupted
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		#clr_country_flag = sgs_selected_battle_fairy_deci
	}
	option = {
		#
		name = sgs.116.1
		custom_effect_tooltip = down_sgs_uprise_middle
		subtract_from_variable = {
			sgs_uprise = 8
		}
		clamp_variable = {
			var = sgs_uprise
			min = 1
			max = 150
		}
		add_war_support = 0.05
		set_variable = {
			ROOT.sgs_doing_days = 20
		}
		set_country_flag = sgs_deci_doing
		hidden_effect = {
			#5tianhou
			random_list = {
				33 = {
					country_event = {
						id = sgs.117						#出现伤亡
						days = 5
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						has_war_support > 0.8
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.2
						check_variable = {
							sgs_uprise > 40
						}
					}
				}
				33 = {
					country_event = {
						id = sgs.118						#新武器亮相
						days = 5
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.8
						num_of_military_factories > 5
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.2
						num_of_factories > 10
					}
				}
				33 = {
					country_event = {
						id = sgs.119						#桑尼来玩
						days = 5
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						neworder > 0.7
						has_political_power > 20
					}
				}
			}
			#10天后
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					country_event = {
						id = sgs.120						#兵王胜利
						days = 10
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.2
						oldorder > 0.2
						has_political_power > 20
					}
				}
				50 = {
					country_event = {
						id = sgs.121						#小队胜利
						days = 10
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						has_army_experience > 15
					}
				}
			}
			#15天后
			random_list = {
				40 = {
					country_event = {
						id = sgs.122						#精彩的决赛
						days = 15
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.3
						has_war_support > 0.6
						has_political_power > 50
					}
				}
				40 = {
					country_event = {
						id = sgs.123						#无聊的决赛
						days = 15
					}
				}
				20 = {
					country_event = {
						id = sgs.124						#争议判罚
						days = 15
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 3
						check_variable = {
							sgs_uprise > 80
						}
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = sgs.125				#比赛结束
				days = 20
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 35
		}
	}
}

					}

				}
			}

						random = 960						# 24*40=960
					}

						days = 10

		not = {

		}
	}
	immediate = {
	}
	option = {
		#给
		name = sgs.146.1
		custom_effect_tooltip = down_sgs_uprise_middle
		subtract_from_variable = {
			sgs_uprise = 8
		}
		clamp_variable = {
			var = sgs_uprise
			min = 1
			max = 150
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = magic_core_a
			amount = 750
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = gun_a
			amount = 750
		}
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = SGS_pay_tension_in_product_idea
			days = 128
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = SGS_mic_spoil0_idea
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SGS_mic_spoil0_idea
				add_idea = SGS_mic_spoil5_idea
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = SGS_mic_spoil1_idea
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SGS_mic_spoil1_idea
				add_idea = SGS_mic_spoil5_idea
			}
			#activate_mission = micFact5_maintain
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = SGS_mic_spoil2_idea
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SGS_mic_spoil2_idea
				add_idea = SGS_mic_spoil5_idea
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = SGS_mic_spoil5_idea
			}
			remove_mission = micFact5_maintain
		}
		else = {
			add_ideas = SGS_mic_spoil5_idea
		}
		add_political_power = 20
		add_stability = 0.1
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
		}
	}
}

								target = CIR
							}
						}
					}

								}
							}

							}

								send_equipment = {
									equipment = magic_core_a
									amount = 500
									target = CIR
								}
							}
						}

			}

			country_event = {
				id = sgs.2181
			}
		}

		}
	}

country_event = {
	#平民逃跑-triggered
	id = sgs.3031
	title = sgs.3031.t
	desc = sgs.3031.d
	fire_only_once = no
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = sgs
	}
	option = {
		#
		name = sgs.3031.1
		set_variable = { global.manpower_escape_from_SGS = 0 }
		
		randomize_variable = {
			var = num_dogs
			distribution = binomial
			min = 0
			max = 1000
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = {num_dogs = 400}
		add_to_variable = { global.manpower_escape_from_SGS = num_dogs } 
		set_temp_variable = { tempv = num_dogs }
		multiply_temp_variable = { tempv = -1 }
		random_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				state_population > 400
			}
			add_manpower = tempv
		}


		randomize_variable = {
			var = num_dogs
			distribution = binomial
			min = 0
			max = 1000
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = {num_dogs = 400}
		add_to_variable = { global.manpower_escape_from_SGS = num_dogs } 
		set_temp_variable = { tempv = num_dogs }
		multiply_temp_variable = { tempv = -1 }
		random_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				state_population > 400
			}
			add_manpower = tempv
		}

		add_stability = -0.08
		#人跑完之后给其他国家加人力，触发事件
		ai_chance = {
			base = 35
		}
	}
}

	#货物送达-小

	desc = sgs.3040.d

		tag = sgs

			has_country_flag = sgs_BLM_failed
		}

			SGS_BLM_cal_remain_for_fake = yes
		}
		
	}
	option = {
		#
		name = sgs.3040.1
		set_variable = {global.sgs_equip_total_temp = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {sgs_current_black_marketer = 1} #河童	
			}
			SGS_buying_from_black_market_repo_kappa = yes
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {sgs_current_black_marketer = 2}
				}
				SGS_buying_from_black_market_repo_fairy = yes
			}
			else = {# 人类
				SGS_buying_from_black_market_repo_human = yes
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = sgs_black_market_repo_preparing_flag
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {sgs_current_black_marketer = 2}
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = SGS_BLM_paying_done_fairy_idea
				days = 30
			}
			else = {
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = SGS_BLM_paying_done_idea
					days = 30
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 35
		}
	}
	option = {
		#零件支付全款
		name = sgs.3040.2
		trigger = {

			check_variable = {SGS_BLM_garbage > 59}

			base = 35
		}
	}

country_event = {
	#加班猝死
	id = sgs.30451
	title = sgs.30451.t
	desc = sgs.30451.d
	fire_only_once = no
	is_triggered_only = no
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 45
		modifier = {
			add = -20
			has_country_flag = SGS_RT_one_resercher_down
		}
	}
	trigger = {
		tag = sgs
		has_country_flag = SGS_RT_reseacher_overtime
		SGS_has_at_least_one_reseach_team_ongoing = yes
	}
	option = {
		#不管
		name = sgs.30451.1
		add_manpower = -1
		set_variable = {sgs_rt_reduce_progress_var = 300}
		if = {
			limit = {
				SGS_reseach_team_one_ongoing = yes
			}
			set_variable = {sgs_rt_changing_team_num = 1}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					SGS_reseach_team_two_ongoing = yes
				}
				set_variable = {sgs_rt_changing_team_num = 2}
			}
			else = {
				set_variable = {sgs_rt_changing_team_num = 3}
			}
		}
		SGS_RT_reduce_progress = yes
		set_country_flag = SGS_RT_one_resercher_down
		ai_chance = {
			base = 35
		}
	}
	option = {
		#停止加班
		name = sgs.30451.2
		add_manpower = -1
		set_variable = {sgs_rt_reduce_progress_var = 300}
		if = {
			limit = {
				SGS_reseach_team_one_ongoing = yes
			}
			set_variable = {sgs_rt_changing_team_num = 1}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					SGS_reseach_team_two_ongoing = yes
				}
				set_variable = {sgs_rt_changing_team_num = 2}
			}
			else = {
				set_variable = {sgs_rt_changing_team_num = 3}
			}
		}
		SGS_RT_reduce_progress = yes
		SGS_RT_close_overtime = yes
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				has_country_flag = SGS_RT_one_resercher_down
			}
		}
	}
}

						country_event = { id = sgs.4023 } #劝人参军
					}
					var:sgs_dove_infl = {
						country_event = { id = sgs.4024 } #劝人复员
					}
					10 = {

				}
			}
		}
	}

		set_variable = { SGS_addition_cond =  40 }
		set_variable = { SGS_change_another =  50 }

		if = {
			limit = {
				or = {
					has_government = oldorder
					SGS_hawk_get_more = yes
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { SGS_addition_cond =  20  }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = SGS_battle_fairy_elite_army
			}
			add_to_variable = { SGS_nego_failed_poss =  100  }
		}
	}
	option = {
		#琪露诺新规线表示必须跟随领袖
		name = sgs.40230.1
		trigger = {
			CIR_army_wait_their_leader = yes
		}

		if  = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = SGS_CIR_uprise_idea
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SGS_CIR_nego_failed
			hidden_effect = {
				random_list = {
					50 = {country_event = { id = sgs.40220 }}
					50 = {country_event = { id = sgs.40221 }}
				}
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = CIR_wait_for_leader_tt
				set_country_flag = CIR_wait_for_leader_solder
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 1 }
	}
	option = {
		#直接同意
		name = sgs.40230.2
		trigger = {
			CIR_army_wait_their_leader = no
			CIR_agree_to_join_as_army = yes
		}
		country_event = {id = sgs.40231 }
		ai_chance = { base = 1 }
	}
	
	option = {
		#犹豫一下
		name = sgs.40230.3
		trigger = {
			CIR_army_wait_their_leader = no
			CIR_agree_to_join_as_army = no
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SGS_CIR_will_nego
		

		random_list = {
			var:SGS_nego_failed_poss = {# 抓起来
				custom_effect_tooltip = SGS_CIR_nego_failed
				hidden_effect = {
					random_list = {
						50 = {country_event = { id = sgs.40220 }}
						50 = {country_event = { id = sgs.40221 }}
					}
				}
			}
			var:SGS_addition_cond = {#追加条件后同意
				custom_effect_tooltip = SGS_CIR_addition_cond_solder
				hidden_effect = {
					if = {
						limit = {  not = { has_government = oldorder } }
						SGS_dove_rise5 = yes
						else = { 
							add_popularity = {
								ideology = oldorder
								popularity = -0.2
							} 
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { has_idea = SGS_battle_fairy_elite_army }
						swap_ideas = {
							remove_idea = SGS_battle_fairy_elite_army
							add_idea = SGS_battle_fairy_elite_army_loose
						}
					}
					country_event = {id = sgs.40231 }
				}
			}
			var:SGS_change_another = {  #换了去向之后同意
				custom_effect_tooltip = SGS_CIR_change_to_worker
				hidden_effect = {
					country_event = {id = sgs.40241 }
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 1 }
	}
}

		trigger = { CIR_peace_task_already_failed = yes }
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = sgs
	}
	option = {
		#直接撵走
		name = sgs.403.1
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = sgs.4031 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SGS_will_arrest_CIR_tt
		ai_chance = { base = 1 }
	}

	option = {
		#来谈判
		name = sgs.403.2
		trigger = { CIR_peace_task_already_failed = no }
		if = {
			limit = {
				#has_government = neworder
				CIR_neworder_way = yes
			}
			country_event = { id = sgs.4032 } #如果桑尼上台而且琪露诺走了斗争线，那么会要求决斗
			else = {
				country_event = { id = sgs.4033 }#直接发布任务
			}
		}

		ai_chance = { base = 1 }
	}
}

	id = sgs.4031

		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SGS_CIR_pulich_task
			not = {has_country_flag = sgs_fear_to_duel_cir_flag}
		}
	}
	desc = {#事前决斗失败，人家直接不合作
		text = sgs.4031.d_duelfail
		trigger = {
			not = {has_country_flag = SGS_CIR_pulich_task}
			has_country_flag = sgs_fear_to_duel_cir_flag
		}
	}
	desc = {#事前决斗失败,合作了但是任务失败
		text = sgs.4031.d_duel_but_fail
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SGS_CIR_pulich_task
			has_country_flag = sgs_fear_to_duel_cir_flag
		}
	}
	desc = {#羁押的时候被琪露诺逃了
		text = sgs.4031.d_voi
		trigger = {
			not = {has_country_flag = SGS_CIR_pulich_task}
			not = {has_country_flag = sgs_fear_to_duel_cir_flag}
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = sgs
	}
	option = {
		#
		name = sgs.4031.1
		#反抗界限减少，加长造核时间
		#set_variable = { SGS.FIR_AREA_CIR_MC_time = 50}
		multiply_variable = { SGS.FIR_AREA_CIR_MC_time = 1.25 }
		round_variable = SGS.FIR_AREA_CIR_MC_time
		custom_effect_tooltip = FA_make_core_time_up
		add_ideas = SGS_CIR_uprise_idea
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = CIR
			}
			add_state_modifier = {
				modifier = {
					resistance_growth = 0.2
				}
			}
		}
		#如果不是任务失败的话还会扣pp
		if = {
			limit = {
				or = {
					not = {has_country_flag = SGS_CIR_pulich_task}
					has_country_flag = sgs_fear_to_duel_cir_flag
				}
			}
			add_political_power = -30
		}

		if = { #如果琪露诺新规，士兵会跟着一起走
			limit = {
				or = {
					has_country_flag =  CIR_wait_for_leader_worker
					has_country_flag =  CIR_wait_for_leader_solder
					not = { has_completed_focus = SGS_face_CIR_army_focus }
				}
				CIR_neworder_way = yes
			}
			country_event = { id = sgs.40311 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = SGS_CIR_army_catched_idea
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { 
					id = sgs.40312
					days = 5
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 1 }
	}
}

country_event = {
	# 安抚结果
	id = sgs.4040
	title = sgs.4040.t
	desc = sgs.4040.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = sgs
	}
	option = {
		#
		name = sgs.4040.1
		set_variable = { var_ok = 70 }
		set_variable = { var_ng = 30 }
		#如果同时妥善解决琪露诺和湖主卫队，则百分之百成功
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = CIR_join_root
				has_country_flag = CIR_army_join
			}
			add_to_variable = { var_ok = 9999  }
		}
		#琪露诺招安失败增加失败概率
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = SGS_CIR_uprise_idea
			}
			add_to_variable = { var_ng = 30  }
		}
		#湖主卫队招安失败增加失败概率
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = SGS_CIR_army_uprise_idea
			}
			add_to_variable = { var_ng = 15  }
		}
		#琪露诺和湖主卫队同时招安失败大大增加失败概率
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = SGS_CIR_army_uprise_idea
			}
			add_to_variable = { var_ng = 70  }
		}
		#激进战场妖精增加失败概率
		if = {
			limit = {
				SGS_peaceful_transit_gov = yes
			}
			add_to_variable = { var_ng = 100  }
		}
		#如果琪露诺走了和平/社民，你还严厉，增加失败概率
		if = {
			limit = {
				or = {
					CIR_guli_way = yes
					CIR_qinwai_way = yes
				}
				has_country_flag = SGS_CIR_strict_NL_flag
			}
			add_to_variable = { var_ng = 20  }
		}
		#如果琪露诺走了和平/社民，你是怀柔，增加成功概率
		if = {
			limit = {
				or = {
					CIR_guli_way = yes
					CIR_qinwai_way = yes
				}
				has_country_flag = SGS_CIR_soft_NL_flag
			}
			add_to_variable = { var_ok = 30  }
		}
		#如果琪露诺走了斗争/威民，你还怀柔，增加失败概率
		if = {
			limit = {
				or = {
					CIR_neworder_way = yes
					CIR_authordemo_way = yes
				}
				has_country_flag = SGS_CIR_soft_NL_flag
			}
			add_to_variable = { var_ng = 25  }
		}


		random_list = {
			var:var_ok = {   country_event = { id = sgs.4041 }  } #安抚成功
			var:var_ng = {   country_event = { id = sgs.4042 }  } #安抚失败
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 1 }
	}
}

	}

		name = sgs.4042.1

		if = {
			limit = {  SGS_peaceful_transit_gov = yes  }
			SGS_dove_rise10 = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {  SGS_sunnystar_post_cw_gov = yes  }
			SGS_dove_rise5 = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = oldorder }
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = oldorder
				popularity = -0.15
			} 
		}
		country_event = { id = sgs.4041 } 

		ai_chance = { base = 1 }
	}
	option = {
		#残酷镇压
		name = sgs.4042.2
		trigger = {
			or = {
				and = {
					has_country_flag = SGS_CIR_strict_NL_flag
					has_idea = SGS_CIR_and_army_uprise_idea
				}
				and = {
					SGS_peaceful_transit_gov = yes
					SGS_hawk_get_more = yes
				}
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {  has_idea = SGS_CIR_new_leader_strict_idea  }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SGS_CIR_new_leader_strict_idea
				add_idea = SGS_CIR_new_leader_forcely_surpress_idea
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {  has_idea = SGS_CIR_new_leader_soft_idea  }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SGS_CIR_new_leader_soft_idea
				add_idea = SGS_CIR_new_leader_forcely_surpress_idea
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = SGS_CIR_forcely_surpress
		country_event = { id = sgs.405  days = 240}
		ai_chance = { base = 1 }
	}
}
